TW: 亞太區 B2B 平衡：該框架通過減少歧義、防止毫無根據的聲明，並使採購決策與經過驗證的證據、適用法律和書面商業條款掛鉤，從而保護買賣雙方。

[t1663]

TW: 2. 詢價(RFQ)與商業審查

[t1664]
EN: Any RFQ, qualification request or automated indication is preliminary. Final acceptance is subject to KYC/KYB, end-use screening, export-control checks, supplier allocation, payment terms and a signed written agreement.
TW: 任何詢價、資格審查請求或自動指示均為初步的。最終接受取決於 KYC/KYB（了解您的客戶/業務）、最終用途篩查、出口管制檢查、供應商分配、付款條件以及簽署的書面協議。

[t1665]

TW: 3. 產品純度與技術適用性

[t1666]
EN: Purity grades, impurity values and processing assumptions are batch-specific. The governing evidence is the released CoA, analytical method, chain-of-custody record and agreed specification. Suitability for a particular end use must be separately validated by the buyer.
TW: 純度等級、雜質值和加工假設均特定於批次。起決定性作用的證據是已發布的 CoA、分析方法、監管鏈記錄和商定的規格。買方必須單獨驗證針對特定最終用途的適用性。

[t1667]

TW: 4. 數據保護与保密

[t1668]

EN: 1. Sustainability Commitment
TW: 1. 可持續發展承諾

[t3118]
EN: YONGYEOKYO Trading House Co., Ltd conducts business through controlled sourcing, documented supplier review, and responsible trade practices. As a supplier of high-purity and ultra-high-purity non-ferrous and rare earth metals, the Company recognizes its role in supporting supply chain integrity, regulatory compliance, and environmentally conscious industrial development.
TW: YONGYEOKYO Trading House Co., Ltd 通過受控的採購、記錄在案的供應商審查和負責任的貿易慣例來開展業務。作為高純度和超高純度有色金屬及稀土金屬的供應商，本公司認識到自身在支持供應鏈完整性、監管合規性以及具有環保意識的工業發展方面所發揮的作用。

EN: 2. Circular Economy
TW: 2. 循環經濟

[t3123]
EN: YONGYEOKYO supports the principles of a circular economy by promoting efficient material use and responsible sourcing practices throughout its supply chain. The Company supports business partners that adopt recycling, recovery, and environmentally responsible operating practices, while avoiding unverified claims regarding recycled content or carbon performance.
TW: YONGYEOKYO 通過在整個供應鏈中促進高效的材料利用和負責任的採購實踐，來支持循環經濟原則。本公司支持那些採用回收、再生和具有環保責任感的運營實踐的業務合作夥伴，同時避免對回收內容或碳排放表現做出未經證實的聲明。

EN: 4. Supply Chain Integrity
TW: 4. 供應鏈完整性

[t3133]
EN: Because YONGYEOKYO supplies high-purity industrial and rare earth materials from Korea into APAC technology supply chains, the Company places particular emphasis on origin transparency, batch traceability, CoA consistency, controlled document release and jurisdiction-specific review. Suppliers are expected to provide accurate supporting records and cooperate with reasonable verification requests.
TW: 由於 YONGYEOKYO 從韓國向亞太地區的技術供應鏈提供高純度工業和稀土材料，因此本公司特別強調原產地透明度、批次可追溯性、CoA 一致性、受控文件發布以及針對特定司法管轄區的審查。期望供應商提供準確的支持記錄，並配合合理的驗證要求。

[t3134]
EN: YONGYEOKYO       ,  ,       .          .

[t3719]
EN: Limitation of Liability
TW: 責任限制

[t3720]
EN: The total aggregate liability of the Seller arising out of or in connection with any contract, delivery, or batch of goods shall in no event exceed the invoice value of the specific batch of goods to which the claim relates.
TW: 賣方因任何合約、交付或批次貨物而產生或與之相關的總責任在任何情況下均不得超過索賠所涉及的特定批次貨物的發票價值。

[t3721]
EN: Under no circumstances shall the Seller be liable for indirect, incidental, special, punitive or consequential damages, including loss of production, loss of profit, loss of contracts, facility downtime, business interruption or reputational damage.
TW: 在任何情況下，賣方均不對間接、偶然、特殊、懲罰性或後果性損害負責，包括生產損失、利潤損失、合約損失、設施停機、業務中斷或聲譽損害。

[t3722]
EN: The Buyer’s sole and exclusive remedy shall be limited to replacement of the affected goods or refund of the invoice value of the affected batch, subject to the RMA & Quality Dispute Policy.
TW: 買方的唯一補救措施僅限於更換受影響的商品或退還受影響批次的發票金額，並須遵守 RMA 和品質爭議政策。

[t3723]
EN: The Seller shall not be liable for delay or failure caused by events beyond reasonable control, including APAC port congestion, customs clearance delay, export/import control action, carrier disruption, force majeure, geopolitical restriction or regulatory intervention.
TW: 賣方不對因超出合理控制範圍的事件（包括亞太地區港口擁堵、清關延遲、進出口管制行動、承運人中斷、不可抗力、地緣政治限製或監管幹預）造成的延誤或故障承擔責任。

[t3728]
EN: Buyer must submit a written claim within 10 calendar days from delivery.

[t3729]
EN: Claim must include batch number, CoA reference, receiving condition, photographs and buyer test results with method declaration.
TW: 索賠必須包括批次號、CoA 參考、接收條件、照片和買方測試結果以及方法聲明。

[t3730]

TW: 材料必須被隔離、未使用並儘可能保存在原包裝中。

[t3731]

TW: 賣方在 48 小時內完成 CoA、可追溯性和內部 QC 日誌審核。

[t3732]

[t3733]
EN: Independent laboratory
TW: 獨立實驗室

[t3734]
EN: Binding Lab Arbitration
TW: 具有約束力的實驗室仲裁

[t3735]
EN: SGS, Eurofins or another mutually accepted ISO/IEC 17025 accredited laboratory acts as neutral analytical authority. Sample split: Buyer retain sample / Seller retain sample / Lab reference sample. Method alignment: GDMS or ICP‑MS as specified in the CoA.
TW: SGS、Eurofins 或其他相互接受的 ISO/IEC 17025 認證實驗室充當中立的分析權威。樣品分割：買方保留樣品/賣方保留樣品/實驗室參考樣品。方法對齊：CoA 中指定的 GDMS 或 ICP-MS。

[t3736]
EN: If Seller fault is confirmed: replacement or refund. If buyer handling, contamination or unauthorized processing is confirmed: claim rejected. If inconclusive: commercial settlement by written agreement.
TW: 若確認賣家有錯：更換或退款。如果確認買家處理、污染或未經授權的處理：索賠被拒絕。如果沒有結果：透過書面協議進行商業解決。

[t3833]
EN: Identify whether mismatch is legal name, registration number, address, plant code or translation/transliteration issue. Cross-check against corporate registry, purchase order, EUC issuer authority and end-use statement.
TW: 確定不符是否為法定名稱、註冊號碼、地址、工廠代碼或翻譯/音譯問題。對照公司註冊、採購訂單、EUC 發行機構和最終用途聲明進行交叉檢查。

[t3834]

[t3837]

TW: 在買方信箋上發布更正的 EUC 附錄，並由授權最終使用者簽署。提交經紀人更正請求並附有解釋備忘錄；將所有版本保留在資料室審計追蹤中。

[t3841]

TW: 檢查韓國/日本保稅庫存中的備用合格批次。如果可能，建議在同一篩選包下進行受控替換裝運；未經買方 QA 批准，請勿更換材料。

[t3850]
EN: Technical deep dive
TW: 技術深入探討

[t3851]
EN: CoA against foundry expectations
TW: CoA 不及代工廠預期

[t3852]
EN: Public TSMC/Samsung foundry impurity limits for specific 7N aluminum lots are generally not disclosed; real buyer specifications are NDA-controlled. Therefore this module compares the CoA to a conservative semiconductor qualification posture: ISO/IEC 17025 lab data, GDMS/ICP-MS, retained samples, contaminant priority list and buyer-specific threshold mapping.
TW: 特定 7N 鋁批次的公​​開台積電/三星代工雜質限值通常不會揭露；真正的買家規格由 NDA 控制。因此，該模組將 CoA 與保守的半導體資格狀況進行比較：ISO/IEC 17025 實驗室數據、GDMS/ICP-MS、保留樣品、污染物優先級清單和買家特定的閾值映射。

[t3895]
EN: Legal trap
TW: 法律陷阱

[t3896]
EN: How a large buyer can bankrupt the supplier
TW: 大買家如何讓供應商破產

[t3897]
EN: If the contract is silent on consequential damages, the buyer may claim line stoppage, lost wafer output, customer penalties, expedited replacement, reputational damage and internal investigation costs. A single delayed or downgraded lot can become a claim far above invoice value.
TW: 如果合約未提及間接損害，買方可以要求生產線停工、晶圓產量損失、客戶處罰、加急更換、聲譽損害和內部調查費用。單一延遲或降級批次可能會成為遠高於發票價值的索賠。

[t3898]
EN: Danger phrase: “Supplier shall be liable for all losses arising from delay or nonconformity.”
TW: 危險短語：“供應商應對因延誤或不合格而造成的所有損失負責。”

[t3899]
EN: Danger gap: no inspection window, no exclusive remedy, no cap, no exclusion of indirect damages.
TW: 危險差距：沒有檢查窗口，沒有唯一的補救措施，沒有上限，不排除間接損害。

[t3900]
EN: Danger evidence: website claims “guaranteed supply” or “zero risk” without contract limits.
TW: 危險證據：網站聲稱“保證供應”或“零風險”，無合約限制。

[t3901]
EN: Protective clause
TW: 保護條款

[t3902]
EN: Limit of Liability — draft wording
TW: 責任限額－措詞草案

[t3903]
EN: Except for fraud, willful misconduct, proven sanctions violation caused solely by Supplier, or breach of confidentiality, Supplier’s aggregate liability arising out of or relating to any purchase order, shipment, delay, nonconforming material, documentation error or related service shall be limited to the amount paid by Buyer for the affected lot. Supplier shall not be liable for indirect, incidental, special, punitive or consequential damages, including loss of production, line stoppage, lost profits, loss of business opportunity, customer penalties or reputational damage, whether claimed in contract, tort or otherwise. Buyer’s exclusive remedy for confirmed nonconforming material shall be replacement, refund or credit for the affected lot, subject to timely written notice, quarantine of the material, and confirmation by an agreed independent referee laboratory.
TW: 除詐欺、故意不當行為、經證明僅由供應商造成的製裁違規行為或違反保密規定外，供應商因任何採購訂單、裝運、延誤、不合格材料、文件錯誤或相關服務而引起或與之相關的總體責任應僅限於買方為受影響批次支付的金額。供應商不對間接、偶然、特殊、懲罰性或後果性損害承擔責任，包括生產損失、生產線停工、利潤損失、商業機會損失、客戶處罰或聲譽損害，無論是在合約、侵權或其他方面提出索賠。買方對已確認的不合格材料的唯一補救措施應為受影響批次的更換、退款或信用，但須及時發出書面通知、對材料進行檢疫並由商定的獨立裁判實驗室確認。

[t3904]
